[30;1m133 | [0m[35m1. **Static type checking** - Parameters have real types that can be checked.[0m
[30;1m134 | [0m[35m2. **IDE support** - Jump to definitions, find references, see docstrings, and use refactoring tools[0m
[30;1m135 | [0m[35m3. **Automatic helptext** - Generated from docstrings and comments.[0m
[30;1m136 | [0m[35m4. **Less boilerplate** - No need to manually define every argument.[0m
[30;1m137 | [0m[35m5. **Hierarchical configuration** - Easily nest parameters in complex structures.[0m
